  - Color scheme: Rose pink (#c2185b) and gold (#bfa14a) accents on a warm
  off-white background

  a "Book Now" button — consistent across all pages
  - Responsive: Mobile hamburger menu, stacking grids, and adjusted typography
  at 768px breakpoint
  - Layout elements: Hero/page banners, card grids, CTA sections, and a 3-column
   footer on every page

  Open index.html in a browser to view the site. All navigation links connect
  the pages together.

❯ change the styling of the website to reflect this branding:**Primary      
  Colors:**                                                                 
  - Rose Gold (#B76E79) - Sophistication and warmth                         
  - Deep Rose (#8B4854) - Richness and depth                                
  - Soft Blush (#F4E6E8) - Gentleness and femininity                        
                                                                            
  **Secondary Colors:**                                                     
  - Champagne Gold (#D4AF37) - Luxury accent                                
  - Sage Green (#9CAF88) - Natural, calming complement                      
  - Cream (#FAF7F5) - Clean, spa-like background                            
                                                                            
  ### Typography                                                            
                                                                            
  **Primary Font:** Elegant serif (for logo and headings)                   
  - Suggests timelessness and sophistication                                
                                                                            
  **Secondary Font:** Clean sans-serif (for body text and practical         
  materials)                                                                
  - Ensures readability and modern appeal                                   
                                                                            
  ### Logo Concept                                                          
                                                                            
  A stylized rose bloom integrated with a crown or elegant flourish,        
  creating a sophisticated monogram. The design should work in full color,  
  single color, and as a simplified icon for social media.

● The logo has been replaced across all 4 pages. Here's what the new SVG logo
  contains:

  Crown (top) -- 5-point champagne gold crown with ball finials at each tip, a
  center jewel in soft blush with a gold border, and an ornamental base band
  with inset rose-gold and deep-rose gems plus decorative gold dots

  Rose bloom (center) -- 4 concentric rings of petals (20 total) with
  progressive gradients from light rose-gold on the outer ring through deep rose
   on the tight inner petals, plus a radial-gradient center bud with a two-layer
   spiral detail

  Foliage (bottom) -- Two large sage-green leaves with midrib veins and
  secondary vein lines, two smaller inner leaves, and a forked stem in muted
  sage

  Flourishes (sides) -- Gold scrollwork curves extending from the leaf tips with
   curled terminals and small gold dot accents

  The SVG renders at 50px wide in the header (40px on mobile) with a subtle
  drop-shadow that deepens on hover. Open index.html in a browser to see the
  full result.

      213            <h4>Quick Links</h4>

❯ ## Brand Overview                                                         
                                                                            
                                                                            
  Rose & Reign is a sophisticated yet approachable hair salon that combines 
  timeless elegance with modern styling expertise. The name evokes natural  
  beauty (Rose) and empowerment (Reign), positioning the salon as a place   
  where clients discover their most confident, radiant selves.              
                                                                            
                                                                            
  ## Brand Personality                                                      
                                                                            
                                                                            
  - **Elegant** - Refined aesthetics and polished service                   
  - **Nurturing** - Caring, attentive approach to each client               
  - **Empowering** - Helping clients feel confident and beautiful           
  - **Knowledgeable** - Expert stylists who stay current with trends        
  - **Authentic** - Genuine relationships over transactional service        
  ### Voice Characteristics:                                                
  - Warm and welcoming, not stuffy                                          
  - Knowledgeable without being condescending                               
  - Encouraging and confidence-building                                     
  - Personal and conversational                                             
  ### Key Messages:                                                         
  1. "Expert care for your crowning glory"                                  
  2. "Personalized beauty that reflects the real you"                       
  3. "Where every client reigns"                                            
  4. "Timeless elegance meets modern expertise"                             
  ### Sample Copy:                                                          
  "At Rose & Reign, we believe your hair should make you feel like royalty  
  every single day. Our expert stylists take the time to understand your    
  unique beauty, lifestyle, and goals—creating looks that bloom with you,   
  not against you."                                                         
  ## Service Philosophy                                                     
  **The Rose & Reign Experience:**                                          
  1. **Consultation First** - Every service begins with understanding the   
  client's vision                                                           
  2. **Customized Care** - No one-size-fits-all approaches                  
  3. **Education Included** - Clients leave knowing how to maintain their   
  look                                                                      
  4. **Premium Products** - Only high-quality, salon-professional products  
  5. **Relaxing Atmosphere** - A sanctuary from daily stress                
  ## Signature Services                                                     
                                                                            
                                                                            
  - **Crown & Color** - Highlighting and balayage services                  
  - **Royal Treatment** - Deep conditioning and repair therapies            
  - **Reign Refresh** - Cuts and styling                                    
  - **Blooming Bride** - Wedding and special event packages                 
  - **Rose Ritual** - Signature scalp massage and treatment                 
                                                                            
                                                                            
  ---## Competitive Advantages                                              
                                                                            
                                                                            
  1. **Personalization** - No assembly-line approach                        
  2. **Expertise** - Continuously trained, experienced stylists             
  3. **Atmosphere** - Luxury without pretension                             
  4. **Relationships** - Genuine connections with clients                   
  5. **Quality** - Never compromise on products or service                  
  6. **Empowerment** - Focus on client confidence and education             
                                                                            
                                                                            
  ---                                                                       
                                                                            
                                                                            
  ## Brand Values                                                           
                                                                            
                                                                            
  **Excellence** - Commitment to superior skill and service                 
  **Authenticity** - Real relationships, honest recommendations             
  **Beauty** - Celebrating diverse definitions of beautiful                 
  **Empowerment** - Helping clients feel confident                          
  **Growth** - Continuous learning and improvement                          
  **Community** - Supporting clients and local connections

  - Rose Gold (#B76E79) - Sophistication and warmth

  - Sage Green (#9CAF88) - Natural, calming complement

  **Primary Font:** Elegant serif (for logo and headings)                   
  - Suggests timelessness and sophistication                                
                                                                            
  **Secondary Font:** Clean sans-serif (for body text and practical         
  materials)                                                                
  - Ensures readability and modern appeal                                   
                                                                            
  ### Logo Concept                                                          
                                                                            
  A stylized rose bloom integrated with a crown or elegant flourish,        
  creating a sophisticated monogram. The design should work in full color,  
  single color, and as a simplified icon for social media.

● The logo has been replaced across all 4 pages. Here's what the new SVG logo
  contains:

  Crown (top) -- 5-point champagne gold crown with ball finials at each tip, a
  center jewel in soft blush with a gold border, and an ornamental base band
  with inset rose-gold and deep-rose gems plus decorative gold dots

  Rose bloom (center) -- 4 concentric rings of petals (20 total) with
  progressive gradients from light rose-gold on the outer ring through deep rose
   on the tight inner petals, plus a radial-gradient center bud with a two-layer
   spiral detail

  Foliage (bottom) -- Two large sage-green leaves with midrib veins and
  secondary vein lines, two smaller inner leaves, and a forked stem in muted
  sage

  Flourishes (sides) -- Gold scrollwork curves extending from the leaf tips with
   curled terminals and small gold dot accents

  The SVG renders at 50px wide in the header (40px on mobile) with a subtle
  drop-shadow that deepens on hover. Open index.html in a browser to see the
  full result.

❯ ## Brand Overview                                                         
                                                                            
                                                                            
  Rose & Reign is a sophisticated yet approachable hair salon that combines 
  timeless elegance with modern styling expertise. The name evokes natural  
  beauty (Rose) and empowerment (Reign), positioning the salon as a place   
  where clients discover their most confident, radiant selves.              
                                                                            
                                                                            
  ## Brand Personality                                                      
                                                                            
                                                                            
  - **Elegant** - Refined aesthetics and polished service                   
  - **Nurturing** - Caring, attentive approach to each client               
  - **Empowering** - Helping clients feel confident and beautiful           
  - **Knowledgeable** - Expert stylists who stay current with trends        
  - **Authentic** - Genuine relationships over transactional service        
  ### Voice Characteristics:                                                
  - Warm and welcoming, not stuffy                                          
  - Knowledgeable without being condescending                               
  - Encouraging and confidence-building                                     
  - Personal and conversational                                             
  ### Key Messages:                                                         
  1. "Expert care for your crowning glory"                                  
  2. "Personalized beauty that reflects the real you"                       
  3. "Where every client reigns"                                            
  4. "Timeless elegance meets modern expertise"                             
  ### Sample Copy:                                                          
  "At Rose & Reign, we believe your hair should make you feel like royalty  
  every single day. Our expert stylists take the time to understand your    
  unique beauty, lifestyle, and goals—creating looks that bloom with you,   
  not against you."                                                         
  ## Service Philosophy                                                     
  **The Rose & Reign Experience:**                                          
  1. **Consultation First** - Every service begins with understanding the   
  client's vision                                                           
  2. **Customized Care** - No one-size-fits-all approaches                  
  3. **Education Included** - Clients leave knowing how to maintain their   
  look                                                                      
  4. **Premium Products** - Only high-quality, salon-professional products  
  5. **Relaxing Atmosphere** - A sanctuary from daily stress                
  ## Signature Services                                                     
                                                                            
                                                                            
  - **Crown & Color** - Highlighting and balayage services                  
  - **Royal Treatment** - Deep conditioning and repair therapies            
  - **Reign Refresh** - Cuts and styling                                    
  - **Blooming Bride** - Wedding and special event packages                 
  - **Rose Ritual** - Signature scalp massage and treatment                 
                                                                            
                                                                            
  ---## Competitive Advantages                                              
                                                                            
                                                                            
  1. **Personalization** - No assembly-line approach                        
  2. **Expertise** - Continuously trained, experienced stylists             
  3. **Atmosphere** - Luxury without pretension                             
  4. **Relationships** - Genuine connections with clients                   
  5. **Quality** - Never compromise on products or service                  
  6. **Empowerment** - Focus on client confidence and education             
                                                                            
                                                                            
  ---                                                                       
                                                                            
                                                                            
  ## Brand Values                                                           
                                                                            
                                                                            
  **Excellence** - Commitment to superior skill and service                 
  **Authenticity** - Real relationships, honest recommendations             
  **Beauty** - Celebrating diverse definitions of beautiful                 
  **Empowerment** - Helping clients feel confident                          
  **Growth** - Continuous learning and improvement                          
  **Community** - Supporting clients and local connections

  - Cream (#FAF7F5) - Clean, spa-like background                            
                                                                            
  ### Typography                                                            
                                                                            
  **Primary Font:** Elegant serif (for logo and headings)                   
  - Suggests timelessness and sophistication                                
                                                                            
  **Secondary Font:** Clean sans-serif (for body text and practical         
  materials)                                                                
  - Ensures readability and modern appeal                                   
                                                                            
  ### Logo Concept                                                          
                                                                            
  A stylized rose bloom integrated with a crown or elegant flourish,        
  creating a sophisticated monogram. The design should work in full color,  
  single color, and as a simplified icon for social media.

● The logo has been replaced across all 4 pages. Here's what the new SVG logo
  contains:

  Crown (top) -- 5-point champagne gold crown with ball finials at each tip, a
  center jewel in soft blush with a gold border, and an ornamental base band
  with inset rose-gold and deep-rose gems plus decorative gold dots

  Rose bloom (center) -- 4 concentric rings of petals (20 total) with
  progressive gradients from light rose-gold on the outer ring through deep rose
   on the tight inner petals, plus a radial-gradient center bud with a two-layer
   spiral detail

  Foliage (bottom) -- Two large sage-green leaves with midrib veins and
  secondary vein lines, two smaller inner leaves, and a forked stem in muted
  sage

  Flourishes (sides) -- Gold scrollwork curves extending from the leaf tips with
   curled terminals and small gold dot accents

  The SVG renders at 50px wide in the header (40px on mobile) with a subtle
  drop-shadow that deepens on hover. Open index.html in a browser to see the
  full result.

      213            <h4>Quick Links</h4>

❯ ## Brand Overview                                                         
                                                                            
                                                                            
  Rose & Reign is a sophisticated yet approachable hair salon that combines 
  timeless elegance with modern styling expertise. The name evokes natural  
  beauty (Rose) and empowerment (Reign), positioning the salon as a place   
  where clients discover their most confident, radiant selves.              
                                                                            
                                                                            
  ## Brand Personality                                                      
                                                                            
                                                                            
  - **Elegant** - Refined aesthetics and polished service                   
  - **Nurturing** - Caring, attentive approach to each client               
  - **Empowering** - Helping clients feel confident and beautiful           
  - **Knowledgeable** - Expert stylists who stay current with trends        
  - **Authentic** - Genuine relationships over transactional service        
  ### Voice Characteristics:                                                
  - Warm and welcoming, not stuffy                                          
  - Knowledgeable without being condescending                               
  - Encouraging and confidence-building                                     
  - Personal and conversational                                             
  ### Key Messages:                                                         
  1. "Expert care for your crowning glory"                                  
  2. "Personalized beauty that reflects the real you"                       
  3. "Where every client reigns"                                            
  4. "Timeless elegance meets modern expertise"                             
  ### Sample Copy:                                                          
  "At Rose & Reign, we believe your hair should make you feel like royalty  
  every single day. Our expert stylists take the time to understand your    
  unique beauty, lifestyle, and goals—creating looks that bloom with you,   
  not against you."                                                         
  ## Service Philosophy                                                     
  **The Rose & Reign Experience:**                                          
  1. **Consultation First** - Every service begins with understanding the   
  client's vision                                                           
  2. **Customized Care** - No one-size-fits-all approaches                  
  3. **Education Included** - Clients leave knowing how to maintain their   
  look                                                                      
  4. **Premium Products** - Only high-quality, salon-professional products  
  5. **Relaxing Atmosphere** - A sanctuary from daily stress                
  ## Signature Services                                                     
                                                                            
                                                                            
  - **Crown & Color** - Highlighting and balayage services                  
  - **Royal Treatment** - Deep conditioning and repair therapies            
  - **Reign Refresh** - Cuts and styling                                    
  - **Blooming Bride** - Wedding and special event packages                 
  - **Rose Ritual** - Signature scalp massage and treatment                 
                                                                            
                                                                            
  ---## Competitive Advantages                                              
                                                                            
                                                                            
  1. **Personalization** - No assembly-line approach                        
  2. **Expertise** - Continuously trained, experienced stylists             
  3. **Atmosphere** - Luxury without pretension                             
  4. **Relationships** - Genuine connections with clients                   
  5. **Quality** - Never compromise on products or service                  
  6. **Empowerment** - Focus on client confidence and education             
                                                                            
                                                                            
  ---                                                                       
                                                                            
                                                                            
  ## Brand Values                                                           
                                                                            
                                                                            
  **Excellence** - Commitment to superior skill and service                 
  **Authenticity** - Real relationships, honest recommendations             
  **Beauty** - Celebrating diverse definitions of beautiful                 
  **Empowerment** - Helping clients feel confident                          
  **Growth** - Continuous learning and improvement                          
  **Community** - Supporting clients and local connections
